msg:The five-star hotel has very good service and is very close to the Zunyi Conference Memorial Hall, which is an enlarged meeting of the Political Bureau of the CPC Central Committee held in Zunyi City, Guizhou Province during the Red Army's Long March in January 1935. This meeting was a major turning point in the history of the Party. The Zunyi Conference Site is a brick-and-wood L-shaped house built in the 1930s. After the Red Army arrived in Zunyi during the Long March, the General Headquarters was set up here.

msg:I blindly selected Phoenix Hotel on Ctrip. The distance from the high-speed rail to the hotel was farther than expected, which was a bit unpleasant. When I arrived at the hotel, the front desk was enthusiastic to check in and also told us about several benefits, but I didn't take it seriously. The hotel is arranged on the 15th floor with a wide view. The decoration of the room is relatively old-fashioned, but the bedding and toiletries are pretty good. The bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas. Although it is facing the street, it is still good to rest at night with the windows closed. The hotel provides laundry, car washing, afternoon tea and supper, all free! These promises actually require a lot of manpower inves**ent, and many hotels are not willing to do it for cost considerations. We didn't try the first three items, but we really went for supper. In the middle of the night, there was only one waiter who cooked noodles, rice noodles, and dumplings. The attitude was very good, the food was hot, and the taste was good. I saw a sentence on the upper right corner of the sign: You deserve to be treated gently, which is really warm. Although the hardware is not as good as some five-star hotels, the service can indeed give five stars.
